< text>
Dr. Morshedi, John, & Catherine all do a great job of making everyone feel welcome while also giving some of the best dental care I've ever received.
Catherine is always a step ahead of any insurance issues and makes every phone call or step in the door feel like you're interacting with family. With Catherine doing as much work on the paperwork side in advance and the efficient working relationship between Dr. Morshedi & John, I'm often in-and-out in 30 minutes for a cleaning.
Make no mistake, though, I've never felt rushed. After a warm welcome from Catherine, she or John start the visit off with a warm and scented neck pillow. The little niceties keep coming through the procedure itself with glasses to help block the bright light of the overhead lamp.
If they have to do any drilling, they offer a radio and headphones to help block that shrilling noise. I found even more comfort in realizing how up to date Dr. Morshedi stays on dental technologies. It sucks to have to get a filling re-done, but, dang it, it was so cool to see her take a 3D image of my mouth and then walk right down the hall to get my new filling off her printer.
Finally, whether it is a standard cleaning or another procedure, the cherry, er, maybe lavender on top, is a fresh lavender-scented towel to wipe off your face. After a quick stop with Catherine to schedule your next appointment, you're out the door feeling calmer than when you stepped through it.< /text>

< Text>
I came in around noon for lunch. Prices were moderate and service was okay. Not much check back check down going on. I decided to have the ribs with fries and baked beans. A side salad for the appetizer. The salad was dripping wet and the water overtook the taste for the buttermilk ranch. When the main dish came the fries were perfect temperature and texture. Beans were lukewarm. Was not satisfied with the beans. And let me get to the ribs; although, I shouldn't have expected much from a Benician Grill, the ribs were dryer than the Sahara desert. If you'd like to dissappoint your parents or don't want that second date this is the place to eat!< /Text>

I would say that they are loosing sales because people (women and girls) just don't want to step into this box and take their cloths off in such circumstances, its bad. OK thats it. <Rating>4<//Rating><Review>I have been to  this restaurant about 5 times, mostly a  popular place for company get togethers. The venue is excellent for large gatherings. Yes they have a bars with variety drink selections. So if you  want a nice place with  food that everyone can enjoy, Mediterranean style with a bit of Persian influence then this is a place to come. They also have pizza which is average when it comes to flavor.  No wow factor in the pizza. The ingredients are good and fresh.  The service is good.  The food in terms of flavoring and execution is average. I have had much better kebabs in many other Persian or Afghani restaurants  throughout the bay area. The marination is simpler and blander in flavor than other places I have been to. But, the quality of the ingredients is good. They have good starters and finger food for those who want to just have something light and drinks in a group.The menu is balanced and does have some good selections for everyone to try. Do I crave to go to this restaurant for the food ever?  Never but if  I had no where else to go ,  yes I would come here to eat as a viable option. My rating for this place is 3.5 but I will  round  it to 4 just for ambience and quality of ingredients plus I cannot give a 3.5 :) rating on google review.</Review>< Pictures>

Stopped here for lunch on our way to Carmel. What a great find. Staff was very welcoming and we were seated right away. They brought out pita bread and cucumber salad then an additional tray of hummus, baba  ganoush and tzatiki. Everything was delicious so far!

Sandwich had avocado, lettuce, tomato and onion with an aioli served on a toasted soft roll. Delicious.

We were glad we made the detour here to have lunch. Yum!< /review>

<Rating>4<//Rating>< review>
I and my wife have long wanted to go to this place, since we live in the apartment right above the restaurant! And finally one night we decided to turn up here. This is quite a unique restaurant in the sense that it caters multiple cuisines - Italian, Persian, American and others.

We decided to try out the chef's soup of the day - a seafood gumbo soup which turned out to be absolutely delicious. As appetizers, we tried out the combo kabab from the usual dinner menu and a kashk-e bademjan based dish from a special menu. The combo kabab had one beef kabab and a chicken kabab which were absolutely delectable, succulent and mouth-watering. One particular aspect that I noticed is that the portion sizes of the kabob plates are smaller than ones in other Persian restaurants in the vicinity (read DishDash, Chellokababi and similar ones). The special entree was a little off-key to our taste.

The service was really great, we enjoyed our time here and the interior is quite classy. I plan to be back here to try the pizzas.</review>
